select count(*) from (select * from (SELECT
					            u.*,
					            d1.DicName UserStatusName,
					            d2.DicName UserTypeName
				            FROM
					            tb_basicuser u
				            LEFT JOIN tb_dictionary d1 ON d1.isdeleted = 0
				            AND d1.DicTypeCode = 'U02000'
				            AND d1.DicCode = u.UserStatus
				            LEFT JOIN tb_dictionary d2 ON d2.isdeleted = 0
				            AND d2.DicTypeCode = 'U01000'
				            AND d2.DicCode = u.UserType
				            WHERE
					            u.isdeleted = 0 ) t3 where 1=1 ) t

select count(*) from (select * from (SELECT
					            u.*,
					            d1.DicName UserStatusName,
					            d2.DicName UserTypeName
				            FROM
					            tb_basicuser u
				            LEFT JOIN tb_dictionary d1 ON d1.isdeleted = 0
				            AND d1.DicTypeCode = 'U02000'
				            AND d1.DicCode = u.UserStatus
				            LEFT JOIN tb_dictionary d2 ON d2.isdeleted = 0
				            AND d2.DicTypeCode = 'U01000'
				            AND d2.DicCode = u.UserType
				            WHERE
					            u.isdeleted = 0 ) t3 where 1=1 ) t

					            u.*,
					            d1.DicName UserStatusName,
					            d2.DicName UserTypeName
				            FROM
					            tb_basicuser u
				            LEFT JOIN tb_dictionary d1 ON d1.isdeleted = 0
				            AND d1.DicTypeCode = 'U02000'
				            AND d1.DicCode = u.UserStatus
				            LEFT JOIN tb_dictionary d2 ON d2.isdeleted = 0
				            AND d2.DicTypeCode = 'U01000'
				            AND d2.DicCode = u.UserType
				            WHERE
					            u.isdeleted = 0 ) t3 where 1=1 ) t

					            u.*,
					            d1.DicName UserStatusName,
					            d2.DicName UserTypeName
				            FROM

				            LEFT JOIN tb_dictionary d1 ON d1.isdeleted = 0
				            AND d1.DicTypeCode = 'U02000'
				            AND d1.DicCode = u.UserStatus
				            LEFT JOIN tb_dictionary d2 ON d2.isdeleted = 0
				            AND d2.DicTypeCode = 'U01000'

					            u.isdeleted = 0 ) t3 where 1=1 ) t

					            u.*,
					            d1.DicName UserStatusName,

				            LEFT JOIN tb_dictionary d1 ON d1.isdeleted = 0
				            AND d1.DicTypeCode = 'U02000'
				            AND d1.DicCode = u.UserStatus
				            LEFT JOIN tb_dictionary d2 ON d2.isdeleted = 0
				            AND d2.DicTypeCode = 'U01000'
